margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.0714em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.5em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size3 size1 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">D</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1433em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.4453em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose nulldelimiter"></span></span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;"><span class="delimsizing size2">)</span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0278em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 1.317em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="arraycolsep" style="width: 0.5em;"></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<p>Thus</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable width="100%"><mtr><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mrow><mi>μ</mi><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>r</mi><mi>d</mi></msub><mo>⋅</mo><msub><mi>g</mi><mi>m</mi></msub></mrow></mtd><mtd width="50%"></mtd><mtd><mtext>(4.9)</mtext></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mu = r_d \cdot g_m \tag{4.9}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">μ</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.5945em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.02778em;">r</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0278em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">d</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">⋅</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">g</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.1514em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0359em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">m</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="tag"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord text"><span class="mord">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">4.9</span></span><span class="mord">)</span></span></span></span></span></span></div>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-3-5-jfet-amplifications">4.3.5 JFET Amplifications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-3-5-jfet-amplifications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>Fig. 4.25 shows JFET amplifier circuit. The weak signal to be amplified is applied between gate and source and amplified output is obtained from the drain-source circuit. For the proper operation of JFET, the gate must be negative w.r.t. source i.e., input circuit should always be reverse biased. This is achieved either by inserting a battery <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi>G</mi><mi>G</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{GG}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">GG</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> in the gate circuit or by means a circuit known as Voltage divider biasing circuit. In the present case, we are providing biasing by the battery <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi>G</mi><mi>G</mi></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{GG}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathnormal mtight">GG</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>.</p>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-2b755ef4.jpeg" alt="img-39.jpeg">
Figure 4.25 JFET amplifier</p>
<p>A small change in the reverse bias on the gate produces a large change in drain current. This fact makes JFET capable of raising the strength of a weak signal. During the positive half of signal, the reverse bias on the gate decreases. This increases the channel width and hence the drain current. During the negative half-cycle of the signal, the reverse voltage on the gate increases. Consequently, the drain current decreases. The result is the small change in voltage at the gate produces a large change in drain current. These large variations in drain current produce large output voltage across the load  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="bold">R</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">L</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathbf{R}_{\mathrm{L}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8361em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathbf">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: 0em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">L</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> . In this way, JFET acts as an amplifier.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="4-3-6-jfet-ac-equivalent-circuit">4.3.6 JFET AC Equivalent Circuit<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-3-6-jfet-ac-equivalent-circuit" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The ac equivalent circuit of JFET is shown in Fig. 4.26. The control of drain current  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">d</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\mathrm{I_d}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3361em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; The current source has its arrow pointing from drain to source to establish a  <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msup><mn>180</mn><mo lspace="0em" rspace="0em">∘</mo></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">180^{\circ}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6741em;"></span><span class="mord">18</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord">0</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.6741em;"><span style="top: -3.063em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight">∘</span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>  phase shift between output and input voltages.</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-6d68a110.jpeg" alt="img-40.jpeg">
Figure 4.26 AC equivalent circuit of JFET</p>
<p>Other Devices</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-3-7-advantages-of-fet-over-bjt">4.3.7 Advantages of FET over BJT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-3-7-advantages-of-fet-over-bjt" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>During 1960s, the electronics industry shifted many electronic applications from the junction transistor to the field-effect transistor (FET), which is easier to manufacture and uses much less power than the junction transistor. Some of the advantages of FET are:</p>
<p>(i) It has a very high input impedance (of the order of <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>100</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">M</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">100\,\mathrm{M}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">100</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">M</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>). This permits high degree of isolation between the input and output circuits.</p>
<p>(ii) The operation of a JFET depends upon the bulk material current carriers that do not cross junctions. Therefore, the inherent noise of vacuum tubes (due to high-temperature operation) and those of transistors (due to junction transitions) are not present in a JFET.</p>
<p>(iii) A JFET has a negative temperature co-efficient of resistance. This avoids the risk of thermal runaway.</p>
<p>(iv) A JFET has a very high power gain. This eliminates the necessity of using driver stages.</p>
<p>(v) A JFET has a smaller size, longer life and high efficiency.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h2 level="2" id="4-3-8-comparison-of-jfet-and-bjt">4.3.8 Comparison of JFET and BJT<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-3-8-comparison-of-jfet-and-bjt" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h2></div>
<p>The JFET differs from an ordinary or bipolar transistor in the following ways:</p>
<p>(i) In a JFET, there is only one type of charge carrier, i.e., holes in p-type channel and electrons in n-type channel are responsible for conduction. For this reason, it is also called a unipolar transistor. However, in BJT, both holes and electrons are responsible for conduction. Therefore, an ordinary transistor is called a bipolar transistor (BJT).</p>
<p>(ii) As the input circuit (i.e., gate to source) of a JFET is reverse biased, it has high input impedance. However, the input circuit of BJT is forward biased and hence has low input impedance.</p>
<p>(iii) As the gate is reverse biased, it carries very small current. Obviously, JFET is just like a vacuum tube where control grid (corresponding to gate in JFET) carries extremely small current and input voltage controls the output current. Hence, JFET is also called a voltage-controlled device. However, BJT is a current controlled device i.e., input current controls the output current.</p>
<p>(iv) A BJT uses base current to control a large current between collector and emitter whereas a JFET uses voltage on the 'gate' (= base) terminal to control the current between drain (= collector) and source (= emitter). Thus a bipolar transistor gain is characterized by current gain whereas the JFET gain is characterized as a transconductance i.e., the ratio of change in output current (drain current) to the input (gate) voltage.</p>
<p>(v) In JFET, there are no junctions along the channel between drain and gate, as in BJT. The conduction is through an n-type or p-type semi-conductor material. For this reason, noise level in JFET is very small.</p>
<p>(vi) The JFET is relatively immune to radiation where as BJT is very sensitive to radiation due to the fact that <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>β</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\beta</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8889em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.05278em;">β</span></span></span></span></span> is practically affected.</p>
<p>Basic Electronics</p>
<p>(vii) JFET has greater thermal stability than BJT.
(viii) The power gain of JFET is much larger than that of BJT at audio frequencies.
(ix) JFET has negative temperature co-efficient at high current levels. It means that the current decreases as temperature increases. This characteristic prevents the JFET from thermal breakdown. BJT, on other hand, has positive temperature co-efficient at high current levels. Hence collector current increases with increase in temperature, which leads thermal breakdown.
(x) Some of the device parameters of JFET and BJT are given below:</p>
<table><thead><tr><th>JFET</th><th>BJT</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>ID=IDSS(1-VGS/Vp)2</td><td>Ic=βIB</td></tr><tr><td>ID=IS</td><td>Ic≈IE</td></tr><tr><td>IG≈0A</td><td>VBE≈0.7V</td></tr></tbody></table>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="4-3-9-fet-applications">4.3.9 FET Applications<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#4-3-9-fet-applications" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<p>The high input impedance and low output impedance and low noise level make JFET far superior to the bipolar transistor. Some of the circuit applications of JFET are:</p>
<p>(i) As a buffer amplifier: A buffer amplifier is a stage of amplification that isolates the preceding stage from the succeeding stage. Because of the high input impedance and low output impedance, a JFET can act as an excellent buffer amplifier (See Fig. 4.27). The high input impedance of JFET means light loading of the preceding stage. This permits almost the entire output from first stage to appear at the Buffer input. The low output impedance of JFET can drive heavy loads (or small load resistances). This ensures that all the output from the buffer reaches the input of the second stage.</p>
<p><img src="assets/images/image-20251223-672fd922.jpeg" alt="img-41.jpeg">
Figure 4.27 Buffer amplifier</p>
<p>(ii) Phase-shift oscillators: JFETs can be used to construct Phase-shift oscillator. The high input impedance of JFET minimize the loading effect in Phase-shift oscillator.</p>
<p>Other Devices</p>
<p>(iii) As RF amplifier: In communication electronics, we have to use JFET RF amplifier in a receiver instead of BJT amplifier for the following reasons:</p>
<p>(a) The noise level of JFET is very low. The JFET will not generate significant amount of noise and is thus useful as an RF amplifier.
(b) The antenna of the receiver receives a very weak signal that has an extremely low amount of current. Since JFET is a voltage controlled device, it will well respond to low current signal provided by the antenna.</p>
<div data-testid="stHeadingWithActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-1p9ibxm e1icttdg2"><h1 level="1" id="solved-problems">SOLVED PROBLEMS<span data-testid="stHeaderActionElements" class="st-emotion-cache-gi0tri e1icttdg3"><a href="#solved-problems" class="st-emotion-cache-yinll1 e1icttdg1"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M15 7h3a5 5 0 0 1 5 5 5 5 0 0 1-5 5h-3m-6 0H6a5 5 0 0 1-5-5 5 5 0 0 1 5-5h3"></path><line x1="8" y1="12" x2="16" y2="12"></line></svg></a></span></h1></div>
<ol>
<li>The intrinsic stand-off ratio for a UJT is determined to be 0.6. If the inter-base resistance is <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>10</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi>K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">10\,K\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07153em;">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>, what are the values of <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\mathrm{B1}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>2</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\mathrm{B2}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B2</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span>?</li>
</ol>
<p>Solution:</p>
<p>Given, <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\mathrm{BB}} = 10\,\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">BB</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span>, <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>η</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0.6</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\eta = 0.6</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">η</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0.6</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Now, <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>2</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\mathrm{BB}} = R_{\mathrm{B1}} + R_{\mathrm{B2}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">BB</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B2</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Or <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>10</mn><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>2</mn></mrow></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">10 = R_{\mathrm{B1}} + R_{\mathrm{B2}}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B2</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Also <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>η</mi><mo>=</mo><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>2</mn></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\eta = \left[R_{\mathrm{B1}} / (R_{\mathrm{B1}} + R_{\mathrm{B2}})\right]</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">η</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="minner"><span class="mopen delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">[</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">+</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B2</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mclose delimcenter" style="top: 0em;">]</span></span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0.6</mn><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mi mathvariant="normal">/</mi><mn>10</mn></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0.6 = R_{\mathrm{B1}} / 10</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0.6</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mord">/10</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Therefore, <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>1</mn></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>0.6</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>6</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\mathrm{B1}} = 10 \times 0.6 = 6\,\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B1</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">0.6</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">6</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>R</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mn>2</mn></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>10</mn><mo>−</mo><mn>6</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">K</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">Ω</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">R_{\mathrm{B2}} = (10 - 6)\,\mathrm{K}\Omega = 4\,\mathrm{K}\Omega</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.00773em;">R</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0077em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">B2</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">−</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord">6</span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">4</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm">K</span><span class="mord">Ω</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<ol start="2">
<li>A unijunction transistor has <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>10</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">10\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span> between the bases. If the intrinsic stand off ratio is 0.65, find the value of stand off voltage. What will be the peak-point voltage if the forward voltage drop in the <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>p</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.625em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span></span></span></span></span>-<span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mi>n</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">n</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.4306em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span></span></span></span></span>-junction is <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>0.7</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">0.7\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.7</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span>?</li>
</ol>
<p>Solution:</p>
<p><span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><mi>η</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>0.65</mn><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace width="1em"></mspace><msub><mi>V</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0.7</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{\mathrm{BB}} = 10\,\mathrm{V}, \quad \eta = 0.65, \quad V_{\mathrm{D}} = 0.7\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">BB</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">η</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord">0.65</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 1em;"></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">D</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.7</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Stand off voltage <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>=</mo><mi>η</mi><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>0.65</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>10</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>6.5</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">= \eta V_{\mathrm{BB}} = 0.65 \times 10 = 6.5\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">η</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">BB</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7278em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">0.65</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span><span class="mbin">×</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2222em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6444em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">6.5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span></p>
<p>Peak-point voltage <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mi>η</mi><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">B</mi></mrow></msub><mo>+</mo><msub><mi>V</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>6.5</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>0.7</mn><mo>=</mo><mn>7.2</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">= V_{\mathrm{P}} = \eta V_{\mathrm{BB}} + V_{\mathrm{D}} = 6.5 + 0.7 = 7.2\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.3669em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">P</span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8778em; vertical-align: -0.1944em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.03588em;">η</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; <ol start="3">
<li>A JFET has the following parameters: <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>32</mn><mtext> </mtext><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I_{\mathrm{DSS}} = 32\,\mathrm{mA}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">DSS</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">32</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">mA</span></span></span></span></span></span>. <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>8</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{\mathrm{GS}}(\mathrm{off}) = -8\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; vertical-align: -0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">GS</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.07778em;">off</span></span><span class="mclose">)</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">8</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span>. <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>4.5</mn><mtext> </mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{\mathrm{GS}} = -4.5\,\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.22222em;">V</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.2222em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">GS</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.7667em; vertical-align: -0.0833em;"></span><span class="mord">−</span><span class="mord">4.5</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.1667em;"></span><span class="mord mathrm" style="margin-right: 0.01389em;">V</span></span></span></span></span>. Find the value of drain current.</li>
</ol>
<p>Solution:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mtable rowspacing="0.25em" columnalign="right left" columnspacing="0em"><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></msub></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub></mfrac><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>32</mn><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>4.5</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>−</mo><mn>8</mn></mrow></mfrac><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup><mtext> </mtext><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr><mtr><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd><mtd><mstyle scriptlevel="0" displaystyle="true"><mrow><mrow></mrow><mi>a</mi><mi>m</mi><mi>p</mi><mo separator="true">;</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>6.12</mn><mtext> </mtext><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">\begin{aligned}
I_{\mathrm{D}} &amp;amp;= I_{\mathrm{DSS}} \left[ 1 - \frac{V_{\mathrm{GS}}}{V_{\mathrm{GS(off)}}} \right]^{2} \\
&amp;amp;= 32 \left[ 1 - \frac{(-4.5)}{-8} \right]^{2}\,\mathrm{mA} \\
&amp;amp;= 6.12\,\mathrm{mA}
\end{aligned}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 7.3992em; vertical-align: -3.4496em;"></span><span <p>Basic Electronics</p>
<ol start="4">
<li>A JFET has a drain current of <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><mn>5</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">5\mathrm{mA}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">5</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">mA</span></span></span></span></span></span>. If <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>10</mn><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">m</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi></mrow></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I_{\mathrm{DSS}} = 10\mathrm{mA}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em; vertical-align: -0.15em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right: 0.07847em;">I</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.3283em;"><span style="top: -2.55em; margin-left: -0.0785em; margin-right: 0.05em;"><span class="pstrut" style="height: 2.7em;"></span><span class="sizing reset-size6 size3 mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mtight"><span class="mord mathrm mtight">DSS</span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">​</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height: 0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right: 0.2778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.6833em;"></span><span class="mord">10</span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathrm">mA</span></span></span></span></span></span> and <span class="math math-inline"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">o</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">f</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mn>6</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">V</mi></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">V_{\mathrm{GS}}(\mathrm{off}) = -6\mathrm{V}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 1em; <p>Solution:</p>
<div class="math math-display"><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>I</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><msub><mi>I</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">D</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><msup><mrow><mo fence="true">[</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mfrac><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow></msub><msub><mi>V</mi><mrow><mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">G</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mtext>off</mtext><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow></msub></mfrac><mo fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">I _ {\mathrm {D}} = I _ {\mathrm {D S S}} \left[ 1 - \frac {V _ {\mathrm {G S}}}{V _ {\mathrm {G S} (\text {off})}} \right] ^ {2}</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height: 0.8333em;
